};\n}\n\n/**\n * Aggregate health check results into an overall status.\n */\nfunction aggregateStatus(checks: Record<string, HealthCheckResult>): HealthStatus {\n  const statuses = sq: \"square\",\n175\t  st: \"street\",\n176\t  ave: \"avenue\",\n177\t  av: \"avenue\",\n178\t  blvd: \"boulevard\",\n179\t  pkwy: \"parkway\",\n180\t  rd: \"road\",\n181\t  dr: \"drive\",\n182\t \"way\",\n189\t};\n190\t\n191\tfunction expandAbbreviations(term: string): string {\n192\t  const lower = term.toLowerCase();\n193\t  if (ABBREVIATIONS[lower]) {\n194\t    return ABBREVIATIONS[lower];\n195\t  }\n196\t  let expanded = term;\n197\t  for (const [abbr, full] of Object.entries(ABBREVIATIONS)) {\n198\t    const regex = new RegExp(`\\\\b${abbr}\\\\b`, \"gi\");\n199\t    expanded = expanded.replace(regex, full);\n200\t  }\n201\t  return expanded;\n202\t}\n203\t\n204\tfunction normalizeForSearch(str: string): string {\n205\t  return str\n206\t    .toLowerCase()\n207\t    .replace(/[^a-z0-9\\s]/g, \"\")\n208\t    .replace(/\\s+/g, \" \")\n209\t    .trim();\n210\t}\n211\t\n212\tfunction stationMatchesQuery(\n213\t  station: Station,\n214\t  normalizedQuery: string,\n215\t  originalQuery: string\n216\t): boolean {\n217\t  const normalizedName = normalizeForSearch(station.name);\n218\t  const expandedQuery = normalizeForSearch(expandAbbreviations(originalQuery));\n219\t  const expandedNormalizedQuery = normalizeForSearch(expandAbbreviations(normalizedQuery));\n220\t\n221\t  if (\n222\t    normalizedName.includes(normalizedQuery) ||\n223\t    normalizedName.includes(expandedQuery) ||\n224\t    normalizedName.includes(expandedNormalizedQuery)\n225\t  ) {\n226\t    return true;\n227\t  }\n228\t\n229\t  const upperQuery = originalQuery.toUpperCase();\n230\t  if (station.lines.some((line) => line === upperQuery)) {\n231\t    return true;\n232\t  }\n233\t\n234\t  const expandedName = normalizeForSearch(expandAbbreviations(station.name));\n235\t  if (expandedName.includes(expandedQuery) || expandedName.includes(expandedNormalizedQuery)) {\n236\t    return true;\n237\t  }\n238\t\n239\t  return false;\n240\t}\n241\t\n242\tfunction scoreSearchResult(station: Station, query: string): number {\n243\t  const normalizedQuery = normalizeForSearch(query);\n244\t  const  }\n250\t\n251\t  if (normalizedName.startsWith(normalizedQuery)) {\n252\t    return 100;\n253\t  }\n254\t\n255\t  const words = normalizedName.split(/\\s+/);\n256\t  if (words.some((word) => word.startsWith(normalizedQuery))) {\n257\t    return 50;\n258\t  }\n259\t\n260\t  if (normalizedName.includes(normalizedQuery)) {\n261\t    return 10;\n262\t  }\n263\t\n264\t  return 1;\n265\t}\n266\t\n267\tfunction buildStationToComplexMap(complexes: ComplexIndex): Map<string, StationComplex> {\n268\t  const map = new Map<string, StationComplex>();\n269\t  for (const complex of Supports brotli, gzip, and deflate based on Accept-Encoding header.\n290\t * Brotli is preferred for best compression ratio.\n291\t */\n292\tfunction compressionMiddleware(): MiddlewareHandler {\n293\t  return async (c, next) => {\n294\t    await next();\n295\t\n296\t    const body = c.res.body;\n297\t    if (!body || c.res.headers.get(\"Content-Encoding\")) return;\n298\t\n299\t    const contentType = c.res.headers.get(\"Content-Type\");\n300\t    if (!contentType?.includes(\"json\") && !contentType?.includes(\"text\")) return;\n301\t\n302\t    const acceptEncoding = c.req.header(\"Accept-Encoding\") || \"\";\n303\t    const contentLength = c.res.headers.get(\"Content-Length\");\n304\t\n305\t    // Skip small responses (not worth compressing)\n306\t    if (contentLength && parseInt(contentLength, 10) < 500) return;\n307\t\n308\t    // Clone response to get the body as buffer\n309\t    const buffer = Buffer.from(await c.res.clone().arrayBuffer());\n310\t\n311\t    // Prefer brotli for best compression, then gzip, then deflate\n312\t    if (acceptEncoding.includes(\"br\")) {\n313\t      const brotlied = await new Promise<Buffer>((resolve, reject) => {\n314\t        const chunks: Buffer[] = [];\n315\t        const brotli = createBrotliCompress();\n316\t        brotli.on(\"data\", (chunk) => chunks.push(chunk));\n317\t        brotli.on(\"end\", () => resolve(Buffer.concat(chunks)));\n318\t        brotli.on(\"error\", reject);\n319\t        brotli.end(buffer);\n320\t      });\n321\t\n322\t      c.res = new Response(brotlied, {\n323\t        status: c.res.status,\n324\t        headers: c.res.headers,\n325\t      });\n326\t      c.res.headers.set(\"Content-Encoding\", \"br\");\n327\t      c.res.headers.delete(\"Content-Length\");\n328\t    } else if (acceptEncoding.includes(\"gzip\")) {\n329\t      const gzipped = await new Promise<Buffer>((resolve, reject) => {\n330\t        const chunks: Buffer[] = [];\n331\t        const gzip = createGzip();\n332\t        gzip.on(\"data\", (chunk) => chunks.push(chunk));\n333\t        gzip.on(\"end\", () => resolve(Buffer.concat(chunks)));\n334\t        gzip.on(\"error\", reject);\n335\t        gzip.end(buffer);\n336\t      });\n337\t\n338\t      c.res = new Response(gzipped, {\n339\t        status: c.res.status,\n340\t        headers: c.res.headers,\n341\t      });\n342\t      c.res.headers.set(\"Content-Encoding\", \"gzip\");\n343\t      c.res.headers.delete(\"Content-Length\");\n344\t    } else if (acceptEncoding.includes(\"deflate\")) {\n345\t      const deflated = await new Promise<Buffer>((resolve, reject) => {\n346\t        const chunks: Buffer[] = [];\n347\t        const deflate = createDeflate();\n348\t        deflate.on(\"data\", (chunk) => chunks.push(chunk));\n349\t        deflate.on(\"end\", () => resolve(Buffer.concat(chunks)));\n350\t        deflate.on(\"error\", reject);\n351\t        deflate.end(buffer);\n352\t      });\n353\t\n354\t      c.res = new Response(deflated, {\n355\t        status: c.res.status,\n356\t        headers: c.res.headers,\n357\t      });\n358\t      c.res.headers.set(\"Content-Encoding\", \"deflate\");\n359\t      c.res.headers.delete(\"Content-Length\");\n360\t    }\n361\t  };\n362\t}\n363\t\n364\t/**\n365\t * Check if a path has a content hash (for immutable caching).\n366\t * Vite produces files like: assets/index-a1b2c3d4.js\n367\t */\n368\tfunction isHashedAsset(path: string): boolean {\n369\t  // Match pattern: /assets/name-[hash].ext where hash is 8+ hex chars\n370\t  return /\\/assets\\/[^/]+-[a-f0-9]{8,}\\.(js|css|svg|png|jpg|ico|woff2?)$/i.test(path);\n371\t}\n372\t\n373\texport function  * Format bytes as human-readable (e.g., \"45.2 MB\")\n542\t   */\n543\t  function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {\n544\t    const units = [\"B\", \"KB\", \"MB\", \"GB\"];\n545\t    let i = );\n\n  /**\n   * Format a timestamp as \"X ago\" for human-readable display\n   */\n  function timeAgo(isoString: string | null): string {\n    if (!isoString) return \"Never\";\n    const ms = < 60) return `${minutes}m ago`;\n    const hours = Math.floor(minutes / 60);\n    if (hours < 24) return `${hours}h ago`;\n    const days = Math.floor(hours / 24);\n    return `${days}d ago`;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Format bytes as human-readable (e.g., \"45.2 MB\")\n   */\n  function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {\n    const units = [\"B\", \"KB\", \"MB\", \"GB\"];\n    let i = 0;\n    while (bytes >= 1024 && i < units.length - 1) {\n      bytes /= 1024;\n      i++;\n    }\n    return `${bytes.toFixed(1)} ${units[i]}`;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Build the HTML response for the /status dashboard\n   */\n  function buildStatusHtml(healthData: {\n    status: string;\n    timestamp: string;\n    uptime_seconds: number;\n    feeds: Array<{\n      id: string;\n      name: string;\n      status: string;\n      lastSuccessAt: string | null;\n      lastPollAt: string | null;\n      consecutiveFailures: number;\n      entityCount: number;\n      lastError: string | null;\n      avgLatencyMs: number;\n      errorCount24h: number;\n    }>;\n    alerts: {\n      count: number;\n      lastSuccessAt: string | null;\n      matchRate: number;\n      consecutiveFailures: number;\n      circuitOpen: boolean;\n      unmatchedCount: number;\n    };\n    delayDetector: {\n      enabled: boolean;\n      activePredictions: number;\n      lastRunAt: string | null;\n    };\n    delayPredictor: {\n      enabled: boolean;\n      modelAccuracy: number;\n      lastTrainedAt: string | null;\n    };\n    equipment: {\n      lastSuccessAt: string | null;\n      outages: number;\n      consecutiveFailures: number;\n    };\n    pushSubscriptions: number;\n    cacheHitRate: number;\n    memory: {\n      rssBytes: number;\n      heapUsedBytes: number;\n      heapTotalBytes: number;\n      externalBytes: number;\n    };\n    failingFeedsCount: number;\n  }): string {\n    const uptimeHours = Math.floor(healthData.uptime_seconds / 3600);\n    const uptimeMinutes = Math.floor((healthData.uptime_seconds % 3600) / 60);\n    const statusColor =\n      healthData.status === \"ok\"\n        ? \"#22c55e\"\n        : healthData.failingFeedsCount >= UNHEALTHY_FEED_THRESHOLD\n          ? \"#ef4444\"\n          : \"#f59e0b\";\n    const statusIcon =\n      healthData.status === \"ok\"\n        ? \"✓\"\n        : healthData.failingFeedsCount >= UNHEALTHY_FEED_THRESHOLD\n          ? \"✗\"\n          : \"⚠\";\n\n    return `<!DOCTYPE html>\n<html lang=\"en\">\n<head>\n  <meta charset=\"UTF-8\">\n  <meta name=\"viewport\" content=\"width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0\">\n  <title>MTA My Way - System Status</title>\n  <style>\n    * { margin: 0; padding: 0; box-sizing: border-box; }\n    body {\n      font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \"Segoe UI\", Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\n      background: #0f172a;\n      color: #e2e8f0;\n      line-height: 1.5;\n      padding: 20px;\n    }\n    .container { max-width: 1200px; margin: 0 auto; }\n    h1 { font-size: 24px; font-weight: 600; margin-bottom: 8px; }\n    .subtitle { color: #94a3b8; font-size: 14px; margin-bottom: 24px; }\n    .status-banner {\n      display: inline-flex;\n      align-items: center;\n      gap: 8px;\n      padding: 12px 20px;\n      border-radius: 8px;\n      font-weight: 600;\n      font-size: 16px;\n      margin-bottom: 24px;\n      background: ${statusColor}20;\n      border: 1px solid ${statusColor}40;\n    }\n    .status-icon { font-size: 20px; }\n    .status-text { color: ${statusColor}; }\n    .grid { display: grid; gap: 20px; }\n    .card {\n      background: #1e293b;\n      border-radius: 12px;\n      padding: 20px;\n      border: 1px solid #334155;\n    }\n    .card-title {\n      font-size: 16px;\n      font-weight: 600;\n      margin-bottom: 16px;\n      color: #f1f5f9;\n    }\n    .metric-grid {\n      display: grid;\n      grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(200px, 1fr));\n      gap: 16px;\n    }\n    .metric { background: #0f172a; padding: 16px; border-radius: 8px; }\n    .metric-label { font-size: 12px; color: #94a3b8; margin-bottom: 4px; }\n    .metric-value { font-size: 20px; font-weight: 600; color: #f1f5f9; }\n    .metric-sub { font-size: 12px; color: #64748b; margin-top: 4px; }\n    .feed-table {\n      width: 100%;\n      border-collapse: collapse;\n      font-size: 14px;\n    }\n    .feed-table th {\n      text-align: left;\n      padding: 12px;\n      border-bottom: 1px solid #334155;\n      color: #94a3b8;\n      font-weight: 500;\n    }\n    .feed-table td {\n      padding: 12px;\n      border-bottom: 1px solid #1e293b;\n    }\n    .feed-table tr:last-child td { border-bottom: none; }\n    .status-badge {\n      display: inline-block;\n      padding: 4px 10px;\n      border-radius: 12px;\n      font-size: 12px;\n      font-weight: 500;\n    }\n    .status-ok { background: #22c55e20; color: #22c55e; }\n    .status-stale { background: #f59e0b20; color: #f59e0b; }\n    .status-circuit_open { background: #ef444420; color: #ef4444; }\n    .status-never_polled { background: #64748b20; color: #94a3b8; }\n    .last-updated {\n      text-align: center;\n      color: #64748b;\n      font-size: 12px;\n      margin-top: 32px;\n      padding-top: 16px;\n      border-top: 1px solid #1e293b;\n    }\n    @media (max-width: 640px) {\n      .feed-table { display: block; overflow-x: auto; }\n      .metric-grid { grid-template-columns: 1fr; }\n    }\n  </style>\n</head>\n<body>\n  <div class=\"container\">\n    <h1>MTA My Way</h1>\n    <p class=\"subtitle\">Real-time subway data system status</p>\n\n    <div class=\"status-banner\">\n      <span class=\"status-icon\">${statusIcon}</span>\n      <span class=\"status-text\">${healthData.status.toUpperCase()}</span>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"grid\">\n      <!-- System Overview -->\n      <div class=\"card\">\n        <div class=\"card-title\">System Overview</div>\n        <div class=\"metric-grid\">\n          <div class=\"metric\">\n            <div class=\"metric-label\">Uptime</div>\n            <div       <div class=\"metric-value\">${healthData.pushSubscriptions}</div>\n          </div>\n          <div class=\"metric\">\n            <div class=\"metric-label\">Failing Feeds</div>\n    <!-- Memory Usage -->\n      <div class=\"card\">\n        <div class=\"card-title\">Memory Usage</div>\n        <div class=\"metric-grid\">\n          <div class=\"metric\">\n            <div ${healthData.feeds\n              .map(\n                (feed) => `\n            <tr>\n              <td>${feed.name}</td>\n              <td><span class=\"status-badge <td>${feed.avgLatencyMs}ms</td>\n              <td>${feed.errorCount24h}</td>\n            </tr>\n          `\n              )\n              .join(\"\")}\n          </tbody>\n        </table>\n      </div>\n\n      <!-- Alerts Status -->\n      <div class=\"card\">\n        <div class=\"card-title\">Service Alerts</div>\n        <div class=\"metric-grid\">\n          <div class=\"metric\">\n            <div class=\"metric-label\">Active Alerts</div>\n            <div class=\"metric-value\">${healthData.alerts.count}</div>\n          </div>\n          <div class=\"metric\">\n            <div class=\"metric-label\">Match Rate</div>\n            <div class=\"metric-value\">${(healthData.alerts.matchRate * 100).toFixed(0)}%</div>\n            <div class=\"metric-sub\">${healthData.alerts.unmatchedCount} unmatched</div>\n          </div>\n          <div class=\"metric\">\n            <div class=\"metric-label\">Last Update</div>\n            <div class=\"metric-value\">${timeAgo(healthData.alerts.lastSuccessAt)}</div>\n          </div>\n          <div class=\"metric\">\n            <div class=\"metric-label\">Status</div>\n            <div class=\"metric-value\">\n              <span class=\"status-badge status-${healthData.alerts.circuitOpen ? \"circuit_open\" : \"ok\"}\">\n                ${healthData.alerts.circuitOpen ? </div>\n            <div class=\"metric-sub\">${(healthData.delayPredictor.modelAccuracy * 100).toFixed(0)}% accuracy</div>\n          </div>\n          <div class=\"metric\">\n            <div     </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"last-updated\">\n      Last updated: ${new Date(healthData.timestamp).toLocaleString()} •\n      <a href=\"/api/health\" style=\"color: #38bdf8;\">View JSON</a>\n    </div>\n  </div>\n</body>\n</html>`;\n  }\n\n  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Health endpoint\n  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  app.get(\"/api/health\", (c) => {\n    // Validate that no unexpected query parameters are passed\n    const query = validateQuery(c, emptyQuerySchema);\n    if (query instanceof Response) return query;\n    const feedStates = getFeedStates();\n    const alertsStatus = getAlertsStatus();\n    const allFeedsOk = feedStates.every(\n      (f) => f.circuitOpenAt === null && f.lastSuccessAt !== null && !f.isStale\n    );\n    const alertsOk = !alertsStatus.circuitOpen && alertsStatus.lastSuccessAt !== null;\n\n    // Count feeds that have been failing for >5 minutes\n    const now = Date.now();\n    const failingFeeds = feedStates.filter(\n      (f) =>\n        f.consecutiveFailures > 0 && f.lastSuccessAt !== null && now - f.lastSuccessAt > 300_000\n    );\n    const unhealthy = failingFeeds.length >= UNHEALTHY_FEED_THRESHOLD;\n\n    const status = allFeedsOk && alertsOk ? \"ok\" : \"degraded\";\n    const httpStatus = unhealthy ? 503 : 200;\n\n    const memUsage = process.memoryUsage();\n    const allMetrics = metrics.getAll();\n\n    // Get cache hit rate from metrics (sum across all label combinations)\n    let cacheHitsValue = 0;\n    let cacheMissesValue = 0;\n    const cacheHitsMap = allMetrics.get(\"cache_hits_total\");\n    const cacheMissesMap = allMetrics.get(\"cache_misses_total\");\n    if (cacheHitsMap) {\n      for (const labeled of cacheHitsMap.values()) {\n        if (labeled.metric.type === \"counter\") {\n          cacheHitsValue += labeled.metric.value;\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    if (cacheMissesMap) {\n      for (const labeled of cacheMissesMap.values()) {\n        if (labeled.metric.type === \"counter\") {\n          cacheMissesValue += labeled.metric.value;\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    const totalCacheRequests = cacheHitsValue + cacheMissesValue;\n    const cacheHitRate =\n      totalCacheRequests > 0 ? Math.round((cacheHitsValue / totalCacheRequests) * 100) / 100 : 0;\n\n    return c.json(\n      {\n        status,\n        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),\n        uptime_seconds: Math.floor((Date.now() - SERVER_START_MS) / 1000),\n        feeds: feedStates.map((f) => ({\n          id: f.id,\n          name: f.name,\n          status:\n            f.circuitOpenAt !== null\n              ? \"circuit_open\"\n              : f.lastSuccessAt === null\n                ? \"never_polled\"\n                : f.isStale\n                  ? \"stale\"\n                  : \"ok\",\n          lastSuccessAt: f.lastSuccessAt ? new Date(f.lastSuccessAt).toISOString() : null,\n          lastPollAt: f.lastPollAt ? new Date(f.lastPollAt).toISOString() : null,\n          consecutiveFailures: f.consecutiveFailures,\n          entityCount: f.entityCount,\n          lastError: f.lastErrorMessage\n            ? f.lastErrorMessage.slice(0, 100).replace(/[\\r\\n]/g, \" \")\n            : null,\n          tripReplacementPeriod: f.tripReplacementPeriod,\n          avgLatencyMs: avgLatency(f.latencyHistory),\n          errorCount24h: errorCount24h(f.errorTimestamps),\n          parseErrors: f.parseErrors,\n        })),\n        alerts: {\n          count: alertsStatus.alertCount,\n          lastSuccessAt: alertsStatus.lastSuccessAt,\n          matchRate: alertsStatus.matchRate,\n          consecutiveFailures: alertsStatus.consecutiveFailures,\n          circuitOpen: alertsStatus.circuitOpen,\n          unmatchedCount: alertsStatus.unmatchedCount,\n        },\n        delayDetector: getDelayDetectorStatus(),\n        delayPredictor: getDelayPredictorStatus(),\n        equipment: getEquipmentStatus(),\n        pushSubscriptions: getSubscriptionCount(),\n        cacheHitRate,\n        memory: {\n          rssBytes: memUsage.rss,\n          heapUsedBytes: memUsage.heapUsed,\n          heapTotalBytes: memUsage.heapTotal,\n          externalBytes: memUsage.external,\n        },\n        failingFeedsCount: failingFeeds.length,\n      },\n      httpStatus as 200 | 503\n    );\n  });\n\n  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Public status page (human-readable dashboard)\n  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  app.get(\"/status\", (c) => {\n    // Validate that no unexpected query parameters are passed\n    const query = UNHEALTHY_FEED_THRESHOLD;\n\n    const status = allFeedsOk && alertsOk ? \"ok\" : \"degraded\";\n    const httpStatus = unhealthy ? 503 : 200;\n\n    const memUsage = process.memoryUsage();\n    const allMetrics = metrics.getAll();\n\n    // Get cache hit rate from metrics\n    let cacheHitsValue = 0;\n    let cacheMissesValue = 0;\n    const cacheHitsMap = allMetrics.get(\"cache_hits_total\");\n    const cacheMissesMap = allMetrics.get(\"cache_misses_total\");\n    if (cacheHitsMap) {\n      for (const labeled of cacheHitsMap.values()) {\n        if (labeled.metric.type === \"counter\") {\n          cacheHitsValue += labeled.metric.value;\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    if (cacheMissesMap) {\n      for (const labeled of cacheMissesMap.values()) {\n        if (labeled.metric.type === totalCacheRequests > 0 ? - SERVER_START_MS) / 1000),\n      feeds: feedStates.map((f) => ({\n        id: f.id,\n        name: f.name,\n        status:\n          f.circuitOpenAt !== null\n            ? \"circuit_open\"\n            : f.lastSuccessAt === null\n              ? \"never_polled\"\n              : f.isStale\n                ? \"stale\"\n                : \"ok\",\n        lastSuccessAt: f.lastSuccessAt ? new -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Metrics export endpoint (for Prometheus)\n  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  app.get(\"/api/metrics\", (c) => {\n    // Validate that no unexpected query parameters are passed\n    const query = -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  app.post(\"/api/security/csp-report\", async (c) => {\n    try {\n      const contentType = c.req.header(\"Content-Type\") ?? \"\";\n      const baseContentType = contentType.split(\";\")[0]!.trim().toLowerCase();\n      const allowed = [\"application/csp-report\", \"application/json\", \"application/reports+json\"];\n      if (!allowed.includes(baseContentType)) {\n        return c.json({ error: \"Unsupported Media Type\" }, 415);\n      }\n\n      const report = await c.req.json().catch(() => null);\n\n      if (!report) {\n        return c.json({ error: \"Invalid report\" }, 400);\n      }\n\n      // Log the CSP violation for security monitoring\n      logger.warn(\"CSP violation detected\", {\n        \"user-agent\": c.req.header(\"user-agent\"),\n        referrer: c.req.header(\"referrer\"),\n        \"x-forwarded-for\": c.req.header(\"x-forwarded-for\")?.split(\",\")[0] ?? \"unknown\",\n        report,\n      });\n\n      // Return 200 to acknowledge the report\n      return c.json({ received: true });\n    } catch (error) {\n      logger.error(\"Failed to process CSP report\", error as Error);\n      return c.json({ error: \"Failed to process report\" }, 400);\n    }\n  });\n\n  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Security disclosure policy (RFC 9116)\n  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  app.get(\"/.well-known/security.txt\", (c) => {\n    const contact = https://github.com/jedarden/mta-my-way/security/policy\\n`;\n    c.header(\"Content-Type\", \"text/plain; charset=utf-8\");\n    c.header(\"Cache-Control\", \"max-age=86400\");\n    return c.text(body);\n  });\n\n  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Real-time arrivals\n  // app.get(\"/api/stations\", (c) => {\n    // Validate that no unexpected query parameters are passed\n    const query = validateQuery(c, emptyQuerySchema);\n    if (query instanceof Response) return query;\n\n    c.header(\"Cache-Control\", STATIC_CACHE_HEADER);\n    return c.json(Object.values(stations));\n  });\n\n  app.get(\"/api/stations/search\", (c) => {\n    const startTime = Date.now();\n    const query = validateQuery(c, stationSearchQuerySchema);\n    if (query instanceof Response) return query;\n\n    const { q } = query;\n    const trimmedQuery = q.trim();\n    const .map((station) => ({\n        station,\n        score: scoreSearchResult(station, trimmedQuery),\n      }))\n      .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score)\n      .map(({ station }) => station);\n\n    const duration = (Date.now() - startTime) / 1000;\n    recordStationSearchDuration(duration);\n    recordStationSearchRequest(results.length);\n\n    c.header(\"Cache-Control\", STATIC_CACHE_HEADER);\n    return c.json(results);\n  });\n\n  app.get(\"/api/stations/:id\", (c) => {\n    const params = validateParams(c, stationIdParamsSchema);\n    if (params instanceof Response) return params;\n\n    const { id } = params;\n    const station = stations[id];\n\n    if (!station) {\n      return c.json({ error: \"Station not found\" }, 404);\n    }\n\n    const (complex) {\n      const complexStations = complex.stations\n        .map((sid) => stations[sid])\n        .filter((s): s is Station => s !== undefined);\n\n      const allLines = new Set<string>();\n      for (const s of complexStations) {\n        for (const line of s.lines) {\n          allLines.add(line);\n        }\n      }\n\n      response.complexId = complex.complexId;\n tripCreateRequestSchema);\n        if (body instanceof Response) return body;\n\n        const {\n          date,\n          origin,\n          destination,\n          line,\n          departureTime,\n          arrivalTime,\n          actualDurationMinutes: providedActualDuration,\n          scheduledDurationMinutes,\n          notes,\n        } = body;\n\n        // Calculate stations[destination];\n        if (!originStation || !destStation) {\n          return c.json({ error: \"Invalid station ID\" }, 400);\n        }\n\n        // Use authenticated user's keyId as owner\n        const ownerId = auth?.keyId || \"anonymous\";\n        const trip = recordTrip(\n          {\n            date: date ?? new Date(departureTime * 1000).toISOString().split(\"T\")[0]!,\n departureTime,\n            arrivalTime,\n            actualDurationMinutes,\n            scheduledDurationMinutes,\n            source: \"manual\",\n            notes,\n          },\n          ownerId\n        );\n\n        if (!trip) {\n          return c.json({ error: \"Failed to record trip\" }, 500);\n        }\n\n        c.header(\"Cache-Control\", \"no-cache\");\n        return c.json({ success: true, trip }, 201);\n      } catch (error) {\n        logger.error(\"Trip recording failed\", error as Error);\n        return c.json({ error: \"Failed to record trip\" }, 500);\n      }\n    }\n  );\n\n  /** Get trips from the journal with optional filters */\n  app.get(\"/api/trips\", requirePermission(\"trips:read:own\" as Permission), (c) => {\n    const query = validateQuery(c, tripQuerySchema);\n    if (query instanceof Response) return query;\n\n    const auth = getRbacAuthContext(c);\n\n    // Non-admin users can only see their own trips\n    const trips = getTrips({\n      ...query,\n      ownerId: auth?.role === \"admin\" ? undefined : auth?.keyId || \"anonymous\",\n    });\n\n    c.header(\"Cache-Control\", \"public, max-age=15\");\n    return c.json({\n      trips,\n      count: trips.length,\n      limit: query.limit ?? 50,\n      offset: query.offset ?? 0,\n    });\n  });\n\n  /** Get a single trip by ID */\n  app.get(\n    \"/api/trips/:tripId\",\n    requireOwnershipOrAdmin(\"trips\", {\n      getOwnerId: (c) => {\n        const tripId = c.req.param(\"tripId\") ?? \"\";\n        const trip = getTripById(tripId);\n        return trip?.ownerId || \"\";\n      },\n      adminBypass: true,\n    }),\n    (c) => {\n      const params = validateParams(c, tripIdParamsSchema);\n      if (params instanceof Response) return params;\n\n      const { tripId } = params;\n      const trip = getTripById(tripId);\n\n      if (!trip) {\n        return c.json({ error: \"Trip not found\" }, 404);\n      }\n\n      c.header(\"Cache-Control\", \"public, max-age=60\");\n      return c.json(trip);\n    }\n  );\n\n  /** Update trip notes */\n  app.patch(\n    \"/api/trips/:tripId/notes\",\n    requireOwnershipOrAdmin(\"trips\", {\n      getOwnerId: (c) => {\n        const tripId = c.req.param(\"tripId\") ?? \"\";\n        const trip = getTripById(tripId);\n        return trip?.ownerId || \"\";\n      },\n    }),\n    requireResourceAccess(\"trip\", \"update\"),\n    auditLogAccess(\"trip\", \"update\"),\n    async (c) => {\n      const auth = getRbacAuthContext(c);\n      const params = validateParams(c, tripIdParamsSchema);\n      if (params instanceof Response) return params;\n\n      const body = await validateBody(c, tripNotesUpdateRequestSchema);\n      if (body instanceof Response) return body;\n\n      const { tripId } = params;\n      const { notes } = body;\n\n      // Pass ownerId for defense-in-depth check (middleware already validated)\n      const ownerId = auth?.role === \"admin\" ? undefined : auth?.keyId || \"anonymous\";\n      const success = updateTripNotes(tripId, notes, ownerId);\n\n      if (!success) {\n        return c.json({ error: \"Trip not found\" }, 404);\n      }\n\n      return c.json({ success: true });\n    }\n  );\n\n  /** Delete a trip from the journal */\n  app.delete(\n    \"/api/trips/:tripId\",\n    requireOwnershipOrAdmin(\"trips\", {\n      getOwnerId: (c) => {\n        const tripId = c.req.param(\"tripId\") ?? \"\";\n        const trip = getTripById(tripId);\n        return trip?.ownerId || \"\";\n      },\n    }),\n    requireResourceAccess(\"trip\", \"delete\"),\n    auditLogAccess(\"trip\", \"delete\"),\n    (c) => {\n      const auth = getRbacAuthContext(c);\n      const params = validateParams(c, tripIdParamsSchema);\n      if (params instanceof Response) return params;\n\n      const { tripId } = params;\n\n      // Pass ownerId for defense-in-depth check (middleware already validated)\n      const ownerId = auth?.role === \"admin\" ? undefined : auth?.keyId || \"anonymous\";\n      const success = deleteTrip(tripId, ownerId);\n\n      if (!success) {\n        return c.json({ error: \"Trip not found\" }, 404);\n      }\n\n      return c.json({ success: true });\n    }\n  );\n\n  /** Get commute statistics */\n  app.get(\"/api/journal/stats\", requirePermission(\"journals:read:own\" as Permission), (c) => {\n    const query = validateQuery(c, commuteIdQuerySchema);\n    if (query instanceof Response) return query;\n\n    const auth = getRbacAuthContext(c);\n    const commuteId = query.commuteId ?? \"default\";\n\n    // Non-admin users can only see their own stats\n    const stats = calculateCommuteStats(\n      commuteId,\n      auth?.role === \"admin\" ? undefined : auth?.keyId || \"anonymous\"\n    );\n\n    c.header(\"Cache-Control\", \"public, max-age=60\");\n    return c.json(stats);\n  });\n\n  /** Get trips for a specific date range */\n  app.get(\n    \"/api/journal/dates/:startDate/:endDate\",\n    requirePermission(\"journals:read:own\" as Permission),\n    (c) => {\n      const params = validateParams(c, dateRangeParamsSchema);\n      if (params instanceof Response) return params;\n\n      const auth = getRbacAuthContext(c);\n      const { startDate, endDate } = params;\n\n      // Non-admin users can only see their own trips\n      const ownerId = auth?.role === \"admin\" ? undefined : auth?.keyId || \"anonymous\";\n      const trips = getTrips({ startDate, endDate, limit: 1000, ownerId });\n\n      c.header(\"Cache-Control\", \"public, max-age=30\");\n      return c.json({\n        startDate,\n        endDate,\n        trips,\n        count: trips.length,\n      });\n    }\n  );\n\n  /** Get journal summary (recent trips + stats) */\n  app.get(\"/api/journal/summary\", requirePermission(\"journals:read:own\" as Permission), (c) => {\n    // Validate that no unexpected query parameters are passed\n    const query = validateQuery(c, emptyQuerySchema);\n    if (query instanceof Response) return query;\n\n    const auth = getRbacAuthContext(c);\n    const ownerId = auth?.role === \"admin\" ? undefined : auth?.keyId || \"anonymous\";\n\n    const recentTrips = getTrips({ limit: 10, ownerId });\n    const stats = calculateCommuteStats(\"default\", ownerId);\n\n    // Non-admin users only get their own trip count\n    const totalTrips =\n      auth?.role === \"admin\" ? getTotalTripCount() : getTrips({ limit: 1000000, ownerId }).length;\n\n    c.header(\"Cache-Control\", \"public, max-age=30\");\n    return c.json({\n      recentTrips,\n      stats,\n      totalTrips,\n    });\n  });\n\n  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Context-aware switching API (Phase 5)\n  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n  // Apply same-origin protection to context operations\n  app.use(\"/api/context/*\", requireSameOrigin());\n\n  /** Get current context and UI hints - scoped to authenticated user */\n  app.get(\"/api/context\", (c) => {\n    // Validate that no unexpected query parameters are passed\n    const query = validateQuery(c, emptyQuerySchema);\n    if (query instanceof Response) return query;\n\n    const auth = getRbacAuthContext(c);\n    const ownerId = auth?.keyId || \"anonymous\";\n\n    // Get context settings (global)\n    const settings = getContextSettings();\n\n    // Admin users get full summary, regular users get scoped data\n    let currentContext: ReturnType<typeof getCurrentContext>;\n    let recentTransitions: ReturnType<typeof getContextTransitions>;\n\n    if (auth?.role === \"admin\") {\n      // Admins see the global context (for system monitoring)\n      currentContext = getCurrentContext();\n      recentTransitions = getContextTransitions(10);\n    } else {\n      // Regular users get their own context if available, otherwise default\n      const userContext = getContextByOwner(ownerId);\n      currentContext = userContext || { ...DEFAULT_CONTEXT };\n\n      // Get user's own transitions\n      const userTransitions = getContextTransitionsForOwner(ownerId, ownerId, 10);\n      recentTransitions = userTransitions || [];\n    }\n\n    const uiHints = getContextUIHints(currentContext.context);\n    const label = getContextLabel(currentContext.context);\n    const icon = getContextIcon(currentContext.context);\n\n    c.header(\"Cache-Control\", \"public, max-age=15\");\n    return c.json({\n      current: currentContext,\n      settings,\n      uiHints,\n      label,\n      icon,\n      recentTransitions,\n    });\n  });\n\n  /** Get context for a specific owner with ownership check */\n  app.get(\n    \"/api/context/owner/:ownerId\",\n    requireOwnershipOrAdmin(\"context\", {\n      getOwnerId: (c) => {\n        return c.req.param(\"ownerId\") || \"\";\n      },\n      adminBypass: true,\n    }),\n    (c) => {\n      const ownerId = c.req.param(\"ownerId\");\n\n      if (!ownerId) {\n        return c.json({ error: \"Owner ID is required\" }, 400);\n      }\n\n      const contextState = getContextByOwner(ownerId);\n      const transitions = getContextTransitionsForOwner(ownerId, ownerId, 10);\n\n      if (!contextState) {\n        return c.json({ error: \"Context not found\" }, 404);\n      }\n\n      c.header(\"Cache-Control\", \"public, max-age=15\");\n      return c.json({\n        current: contextState,\n        settings: getContextSettings(),\n        uiHints: getContextUIHints(contextState.context),\n        label: getContextLabel(contextState.context),\n        icon: getContextIcon(contextState.context),\n        recentTransitions: transitions || [],\n      });\n    }\n  );\n\n  /** Detect context from request parameters */\n  app.post(\n    \"/api/context/detect\",\n    requireResourceAccess(\"context\", \"create\"),\n    requirePermission(\"predictions:create\" as Permission),\n    async (c) => {\n      try {\n        const auth = getRbacAuthContext(c);\n        const body = await validateBody(c, contextDetectRequestSchema);\n        if (body instanceof Response) return body;\n\n        // Get owner ID from auth context - users can only detect context for themselves\n        const ownerId = auth?.keyId || \"anonymous\";\n\n        // tapHistory in the API schema uses a different shape than FavoriteTapEvent;\n        // location-based detection is sufficient server-side.\n        const context = detectContextFromRequest({\n          latitude: body.latitude,\n          longitude: body.longitude,\n          currentScreen: body.currentScreen,\n          screenTime: body.screenTime,\n          recentActions: body.recentActions,\n        });\n\n        // Store context with ownership - always use authenticated user's ID\n        const { context: detectedContext } = detectAndUpdateContextWithOwner(\n          {\n            nearStation: context.factors.location.nearStation,\n            nearStationId: context.factors.location.stationId,\n            distanceToStation: context.factors.location.distance,\n            tapHistory: [],\n            currentScreen: body.currentScreen || \"home\",\n            screenTime: body.screenTime || 0,\n            recentActions: body.recentActions || [],\n          },\n          ownerId\n        );\n\n        c.header(\"Cache-Control\", \"no-cache\");\n        return c.json({ context: detectedContext });\n      } catch (err) {\n        logger.error(\"Context detection failed\", err as Error);\n        return c.json(\n          {\n            error: \"Failed to detect context\",\n            message: err instanceof Error ? err.message : \"Unknown error\",\n          },\n          500\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  );\n\n  /** Set manual context override */\n  app.post(\n    \"/api/context/override\",\n    requireResourceAccess(\"context\", \"update\"),\n    requirePermission(\"predictions:create\" as Permission),\n    auditLogAccess(\"context\", \"update\"),\n    async (c) => {\n      try {\n        const auth = getRbacAuthContext(c);\n        const body = await validateBody(c, contextOverrideRequestSchema);\n        if (body instanceof Response) return body;\n\n        const { context } = body;\n        const ownerId = auth?.keyId || \"anonymous\";\n\n        // Store context with ownership - always use authenticated user's ID\n        const { context: newContext } = detectAndUpdateContextWithOwner(\n          {\n            nearStation: false,\n            tapHistory: [],\n            currentScreen: \"home\",\n            screenTime: 0,\n            recentActions: [],\n            manualOverride: context,\n          },\n          ownerId\n        );\n\n        c.header(\"Cache-Control\", \"no-cache\");\n        return c.json({ success: true, context: newContext });\n      } catch (error) {\n        logger.error(\"Context override failed\", error as Error);\n        return c.json({ error: \"Failed to set context override\" }, 500);\n      }\n    }\n  );\n\n  /** Clear manual context override - requires authentication */\n  app.post(\n    \"/api/context/clear\",\n    requireResourceAccess(\"context\", \"update\"),\n    requirePermission(\"predictions:create\" as Permission),\n    auditLogAccess(\"context\", \"update\"),\n    async (c) => {\n      const auth = getRbacAuthContext(c);\n      const body = await validateBody(c, contextClearRequestSchema);\n      if (body instanceof Response) return body;\n\n      // Get owner ID from auth context\n      const ownerId = auth?.keyId || \"anonymous\";\n\n      // Clear manual override for authenticated user only (owner-scoped)\n      const context = clearManualOverrideForOwner(ownerId);\n\n      logger.info(\"Manual context override cleared\", { ownerId });\n\n      c.header(\"Cache-Control\", \"no-cache\");\n      return c.json({ success: true, context });\n    }\n  );\n\n  /** Update context settings - admin only */\n  app.patch(\n    \"/api/context/settings\",\n    requireRole(\"admin\"),\n    requireAdmin(),\n    auditLogAccess(\"context\", \"update\"),\n    async (c) => {\n      try {\n        const body = await validateBody(c, contextSettingsUpdateRequestSchema);\n        if (body instanceof Response) return body;\n\n        updateContextSettings(body);\n\n        return c.json({ success: true, settings: 500);\n      }\n    }\n  );\n\n  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // OAuth 2.0 Authentication - DISABLED: Feature not used by frontend\n  // These
